<div id="review_96738606" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/96738606" />
    <a title="Bella Mcfarland" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3529895-bella-mcfarland"><img alt="Bella Mcfarland" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/96738606?book_show_action=true">Apr 01, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bella Mcfarland" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bella Mcfarland" href="/user/show/3529895-bella-mcfarland">Bella Mcfarland</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer96738606" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16269833789611713918">Let me start by saying I love anything and everything written by Jennifer Laurens. She masterfully crafts love stories that are believable and leaves you hungering for more. Her characters are usually well-developed and you can’t wait to know what happens next.<br/><br/>Penitence is book 2 in the Heavenly Series and I admit I couldn’t put it down. It begins with Zoe at the hospital. She just came back from the dead, literally yanked from the arms of the angel she loves, her Guardian Angel-Matthias. She is</span>
  <span id="freeText16269833789611713918" style="display:none">Let me start by saying I love anything and everything written by Jennifer Laurens. She masterfully crafts love stories that are believable and leaves you hungering for more. Her characters are usually well-developed and you can’t wait to know what happens next.<br /><br />Penitence is book 2 in the Heavenly Series and I admit I couldn’t put it down. It begins with Zoe at the hospital. She just came back from the dead, literally yanked from the arms of the angel she loves, her Guardian Angel-Matthias. She is in so much pain, but soon realizes the worst is yet to come—Matthias is longer her Guardian. <br /><br />Instead two men enter Zoe’s life—Weston, her friend’s ex boyfriend who pursues her until she agrees to go out with him, and Albert, a being she believes is her new Guardian Angel. Albert turns out to be the devil’s spawn, a demon after her soul. Finally, Matthias returns but not to be her guardian. He warns her about Albert, who just happens to be his very evil father.<br /><br />Soon Zoe is fighting off Albert’s evil intention and his tendency to use her friends and family against her. We watch her grow and become stronger as a person. She’s also caught in a love triangle with Matthias and Weston. I’m definitely Team Matthias!!! <br /><br />It takes skills to make a reader get lost in a character and Ms. Laurens has it. I felt Zoe’s pain as she struggled with Matthias’ absence at the beginning of the book and later as she fought off Albert and his evil agenda, felt Zoe’s awkwardness as she went back to school and faced gawking students, the stress of dealing with autistic sister and her pothead brother, a jealous ex-BFF and even the death of a student. This book has everything, romance, mystery, teen angst….<br /><br />Lauren is a fabulous writer, and I found find myself staying up late to finish the book. My ultimate disappointment is I must wait for the third installment to come out. If you haven’t bought your copy of Penitence, do so now. It was worth the wait.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16269833789611713918" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/105865909" />
    <a title="Lili" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2463287-lili"><img alt="Lili" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489340894p2/2463287.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/105865909?book_show_action=true">Jun 06, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lili" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lili" href="/user/show/2463287-lili">Lili</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2463287-lili?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2463287-lili?shelf=ya-fantasy">ya-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer105865909" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8842242144007460713">After spending about two weeks recovering in the hospital after a terrible accident, Zoe Dodd decides to start life with a different approach. When her previous guardian angel disappears, she's left more confused than ever. Keeping up with the surroundings happening in her current life take a back seat to the thoughts and sights that Zoe now experiences with a new view. Getting a new guardian angel is the last thing she expects, and when she knows who and what he really is she's gets more questi</span>
  <span id="freeText8842242144007460713" style="display:none">After spending about two weeks recovering in the hospital after a terrible accident, Zoe Dodd decides to start life with a different approach. When her previous guardian angel disappears, she's left more confused than ever. Keeping up with the surroundings happening in her current life take a back seat to the thoughts and sights that Zoe now experiences with a new view. Getting a new guardian angel is the last thing she expects, and when she knows who and what he really is she's gets more questions than answers. As she contemplates what this new "angel" might bring upon her world, she slowly sees signs of her life becoming more dangerous by the minute.<br /><br />In this sequel of Zoe's life touched by the spiritual, Penitence brings more background on it's cast of characters, and adds a new one that's yet to be dealt with. More somber than Heavenly, Penitence digs deeper into Matthias' past, and progresses in Zoe's friendships and blossoming relationships.<br /><br /><br />Having tasted an entrancing debut with Heavenly, Penitence was just made to add to the growing suspense of future actions in Zoe's life. Dealing with her family and friends intermingles with her daily dose of dealing with the spiritual. I loved the way Laurens really developed the cast of characters in this book. She was able to explain through voices and actions the reasons for some past occurrences and build up to the present challenging events. What was deeply unexpected was Zoe's internal chaos of sensations that was the result when she slowly realized there's more to the people around her than she originally thought. It was a refreshing wave of something new in an already deeply touching tale. Leaving off on a cliffhanger just added to the thrill of waiting for the third installment in the Heavenly series, Absolution.<br /><br /><br />Quotes:<br /><br />"You're the first girl who's had the guts to touch my controls." --pg. 234<br /><br /><br /><br />Grade: A</span>
  <a data-text-id="8842242144007460713" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_109840716" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/109840716" />
    <a title="Stephanie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3043110-stephanie"><img alt="Stephanie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489429470p2/3043110.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/109840716?book_show_action=true">Jul 03, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stephanie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stephanie" href="/user/show/3043110-stephanie">Stephanie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3043110-stephanie?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3043110-stephanie?shelf=review-book">review-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3043110-stephanie?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer109840716" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13478566728551725467">In this stunning sequel to Heavenly, Zoe’s true love and guardian angel, Matthias, has disappeared, and in his place, an evil spirit has appeared who is trying to capture her soul and destroy those around her. Her family still faces their normal difficulties with her brother’s drug abuse and her sister’s autism, and her best friend, Britt hates her now too, since her old boyfriend has fallen in love with Zoe and a relationship has ensued. When Matthias finally returns, will things go back to the</span>
  <span id="freeText13478566728551725467" style="display:none">In this stunning sequel to Heavenly, Zoe’s true love and guardian angel, Matthias, has disappeared, and in his place, an evil spirit has appeared who is trying to capture her soul and destroy those around her. Her family still faces their normal difficulties with her brother’s drug abuse and her sister’s autism, and her best friend, Britt hates her now too, since her old boyfriend has fallen in love with Zoe and a relationship has ensued. When Matthias finally returns, will things go back to the way they were, or will the evil spirit destroy them all?<br /><br />Wow, what a great sequel! I loved delving back into the story of Zoe and Matthias whose unearthly love first captivated me in Heavenly. If you haven’t read Heavenly, I highly recommend you do, and on that note, Penitence is not really a standalone novel. You should certainly read its predecessor first in order to fully understand this one. This story was really gripping with lots of excitement. While the love between Zoe and Matthias is so intriguing, I think it was really cool that the author added a whole new aspect in this book, in that the main storyline was the evil spirit who was essentially stalking Zoe around, trying to capture her soul and force her into evilness (and wait until you find out who he is!). I also thought it was a great twist that she added another love interest into the story, in that Zoe begins dating another guy, but feels conflicted because of her love for Matthias. This book definitely kept me turning the pages, and I’m looking forward to the next one in the series!<br /><br />A really great sequel! Angels, spirits, romance! I think you should check this series out if you’re looking for something a little different.<br /><br />Note: I received a copy of this book in exchange for an honest review.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_96578578" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/96578578" />
    <a title="Amber  ~ The Reading Addict" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3172251-amber-the-reading-addict"><img alt="Amber  ~ The Reading Addict" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1493927899p2/3172251.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/96578578?book_show_action=true">Mar 31, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amber  ~ The Reading Addict" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amber  ~ The Reading Addict" href="/user/show/3172251-amber-the-reading-addict">Amber  ~ The Reading Addict</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer96578578" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8405221912929563207">The first book in this series, Heavenly, is one of my favorite books. I loved everything about it. From the plot to the characters, Heavenly is truly breathtaking. Penitence is just as amazing and heart-wrenching. The story takes a surprising turn but is still just as powerful and thought provoking. <br/><br/>From the very beginning of the book, I was swept away by a tidal wave of emotions. Zoe is such a normal, relatable character. I could easily place myself in her shoes and see things through her eyes.</span>
  <span id="freeText8405221912929563207" style="display:none">The first book in this series, Heavenly, is one of my favorite books. I loved everything about it. From the plot to the characters, Heavenly is truly breathtaking. Penitence is just as amazing and heart-wrenching. The story takes a surprising turn but is still just as powerful and thought provoking. <br /><br />From the very beginning of the book, I was swept away by a tidal wave of emotions. Zoe is such a normal, relatable character. I could easily place myself in her shoes and see things through her eyes. Her strength and wit make her a good role model for teens, as well as someone I could admire. <br /><br />Ah, Matthias. I loved how pure and honest he was. I get so tired of authors spinning tales of bad boys with "deep, dark secrets." For once, the main character's romantic interest is someone who is actually good for her. Matthias' character was one of the major contributors to my love of this series. I found myself missing him as much as Zoe did when he wasn't around. <br /><br />Once again, Lauren's novel is not only about romance or supernatural occurrences. The novel places heavy focus on the pain and heartache that come with having a autistic child in the family, as well as the roller coaster of dealing with drug addictions. There were times when I felt my heart would burst from the love and pain that Zoe and her family shared. As I said in my review of Heavenly, it was refreshing to read a book about such a tightly-knit family. <br /><br />I would definitely recommend this book. Penitence is one novel that I will be reading over and over again. Powerful and moving, this novel will sweep you off of your feet and redefine the meaning of unconditional love.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8405221912929563207" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer1926211500990482761">Jennifer, aka JM Warwick was born and raised in Southern California and her hometown of Palos Verdes Estates flavors her books: A Season of Eden and An Open Vein. She doesn't limit herself to writing one genre, and was the first to author four romance novels centered around the popular sport of ballroom dancing.She has YA novels published under her YA romance name of Jennifer Laurens: Falling for </span>
  <span id="freeText1926211500990482761" style="display:none">Jennifer, aka JM Warwick was born and raised in Southern California and her hometown of Palos Verdes Estates flavors her books: A Season of Eden and An Open Vein. She doesn't limit herself to writing one genre, and was the first to author four romance novels centered around the popular sport of ballroom dancing.She has YA novels published under her YA romance name of Jennifer Laurens: Falling for Romeo, Magic Hands, Nailed and the Heavenly series: Heavenly ( 2009) Penitence (2010) and Absolution (2010) A Season of Eden (2011) and Overprotected ( 2011 ) Grace Doll ( 2012 ) .An Open Vein is under her JM Warwick pen name. Jennifer lives in Utah and has 6 children, one of whom has autism. Jennifer doesn't put stock in reviews - in fact she never reads them.</span>
